same spiel: After a couple of years together, you both have to start making an effort to keep the ol' fire burning. (No pressure, right?)</p>\n<p>Shopping thoughtfully for your wife's gifts is one way to tend to that aspect of your relationship, whether you're celebrating an <a href=\"https://mashable.com/gifts/best-anniversary-gifts-for-her/?utm_campaign&#38;utm_context=textlink&#38;utm_medium=rss&#38;utm_source\"><ins>anniversary</ins></a>, a holiday, or treating her just for kicks. But this is often easier said than done, because you have to do your research. (See also: pay attention.) What are her hobbies? What gets her excited? Facebook and Twitter to take action before the U.S. presidential election on November 3.</p>\n<p>Specifically, Mozilla is demanding the two social media giants help &#8220;<a href=\"https://www.mozilla.org/en-US/firefox/unfck/?utm_content=bufferd6cc0&#38;utm_medium=social&#38;utm_source=twitter&#38;utm_campaign=unfck\"><ins>unfck the internet</ins></a>&#8221; by making big changes to two major features on the Facebook and Twitter platforms.</p>\n<p>On Tuesday, Mozilla <a href=\"https://foundation.mozilla.org/en/blog/mozilla-urges-facebook-and-twitter-halt-dangerous-recommendations/\"><ins>published</ins></a> an open letter in a <a href=\"https://assets.mofoprod.net/network/images/MoFo_WaPo-Open-Letter-092020-v72x.original.png\"><ins>full-page ad</ins></a> in the <em>Washington Post</em> urging Facebook to turn off its Group recommendations feature prior to the November elections.
